[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m150[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mmemmove[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&wIn[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, &wIn[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnChan-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsUInt16Number[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m151[0m[39m:        wIn[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mnChan-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = tmp;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m152[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m153[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m154[0m[39m:    return accum;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mcmsUNUSED_PARAMETER[0m[1;39m([0m[39minfo[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mcmsUNUSED_PARAMETER[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStride[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m159[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack-buffer-overflow occurs in `CreateNamedColorDevicelink` [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`src/cmsvirt.[0m[1;92mc:1066[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1114[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m due to a critical issue: **the return value of [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cmsChangeBuffersFormat` is not checked, and a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte buffer is used when the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatter may expect more bytes**.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### The Vulnerability Chain:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m1071[0m[39m**: `cmsUInt32Number i` is declared [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m1097[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1099[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mcmsChangeBuffersFormat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform, TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOutputFormat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called WITHOUT checking the return value[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m1103[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mcmsDoTransform[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform, &i, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` passes the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte buffer `&i` as[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why the Overflow Occurs:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `cmsChangeBuffersFormat` can fail and return FALSE if:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The transform doesn't have `cmsFLAGS_CAN_CHANGE_FORMATTER` flag[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The formatter lookup fails[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When it fails, the transform retains its **previous InputFormat and FromInput [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatter**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The previous formatter may expect more bytes than TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When `UnrollChunkyBytes` is called with the old InputFormat, it extracts `nChan` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom that format[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `nChan > [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor with extra channels[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it reads beyond the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The read at line [0m[1;36m130[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`v = [0m[1;35mFROM_8_TO_16[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*accum[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggers the overflow at offset[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Check Return Value and Use Proper Buffer Type[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify `src/cmsvirt.c` in the `CreateNamedColorDevicelink` function:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Change the variable declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1071[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Split the declaration into separate lines for clarity[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a `cmsUInt16Number` variable to hold the named color index properly[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Add error checking for `cmsChangeBuffersFormat` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1099[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check if the function returns FALSE[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If it fails, jump to the Error label to properly clean up[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Update the transform loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1102[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1104[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use the properly-sized `cmsUInt16Number` variable instead of the loop counter [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddress[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures the input buffer matches TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Implementation Steps:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Locate `CreateNamedColorDevicelink` in `src/cmsvirt.c` starting at line[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1066[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Modify the variable declarations at line [0m[1;36m1071[0m[39m:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m OLD:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcmsUInt32Number i, nColors;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m NEW:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcmsUInt32Number i, nColors;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcmsUInt16Number namedColorIndex;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: After the `cmsChangeBuffersFormat` call [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1099[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add error [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Make sure we have proper formatters[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcmsChangeBuffersFormat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform, TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX,[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mFLOAT_SH[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;35mCOLORSPACE_SH[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35m_cmsLCMScolorSpace[0m[1;39m([0m[39mv ->ExitColorSpace[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    | [0m[1;35mBYTES_SH[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;35mCHANNELS_SH[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsChannelsOfColorSpace[0m[1;39m([0m[39mv ->ExitColorSpace[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto Error;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m**: Modify the transform loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1102[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1104[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Apply the transform to colorants.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < nColors; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    namedColorIndex = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsUInt16Number[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mcmsDoTransform[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform, &namedColorIndex, nc2 ->List[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.DeviceColorant, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix Is Optimal:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses the root cause**: Ensures the formatter change succeeds before using[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe transform[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Type safety**: Uses the correct data type [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsUInt16Number[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for named color [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Buffer size correctness**: The input buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now matches what [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX expects[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Follows existing patterns**: Uses the established error handling pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgoto[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mError[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already present in the function[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Minimal changes**: Only modifies the problematic function without affecting [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe broader codebase[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Preserves functionality**: Even if `cmsChangeBuffersFormat` succeeds and uses [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Unroll1Word` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich reads [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the fix ensures the buffer is properly sized[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The named color iteration logic remains unchanged[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error handling flow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mError label cleanup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is already present and reused[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The transform application semantics are preserved[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The output colorant population works identically[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing tests and use cases remain supported[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **New failure path**: If `cmsChangeBuffersFormat` fails, the function now [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns NULL instead of potentially crashing[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the correct behavior - failing gracefully is better [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan buffer overflow[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Callers already handle NULL returns from this function[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Type casting**: The cast from `i` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsUInt32Number[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to `namedColorIndex` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcmsUInt16Number[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Named color lists are limited to [0m[1;36m65535[0m[39m colors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmsUInt16Number[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrange[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so truncation won't occur in practice[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The original code already assumed indices fit in the named color range[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLooking at similar patterns, the codebase consistently:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Checks return values of functions that can fail [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike `cmsWriteTag` at line [0m[1;36m1106[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses goto Error for cleanup [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1084[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1087[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1091[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1106[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Handles buffer sizing carefully in formatter operations[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix aligns with these established patterns and best practices in the lcms [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: `UnrollChunkyBytes` function in `[0m[35m/src/lcms/src/[0m[95mcmspack.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m130:13[0m[39m`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Type**: READ of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at address [0m[1;36m0x7fbd4a160d24[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Severity**: SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m27[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-stack-buffer-overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Call stack**: The overflow originated from `cmsTransform2DeviceLink` → [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CreateNamedColorDevicelink` → `cmsDoTransform` → `CachedXFORM` → [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UnrollChunkyBytes`[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer shadow bytes indicated:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m36[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[32m'i.i'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1071[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m <== Memory access at offset [0m[1;36m36[0m[39m overflows this variable[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis shows that a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte variable allocated at stack offset [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m36[0m[39m was being [0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused as input to `cmsDoTransform`, which expected a specific format based on [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch made three key changes to `[0m[35m/src/lcms/src/[0m[95mcmsvirt.c[0m[39m`:[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcmsChangeBuffersFormat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxform, TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX,[0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Changed the transform call** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1105[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1106[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe rationale appears to be that `TYPE_NAMED_COLOR_INDEX` with `[0m[1;35mBYTES_SH[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Post-Patch Results[0m                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory management in cmsvirt.c**: A comprehensive audit of all allocation and [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `nc2` is allocated at line [0m[1;36m1090[0m[39m via `[0m[1;35mcmsDupNamedColorList[0m[1;39m([0m[39mOriginal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `cmsAllocNamedColorList` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcell [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m frees on error: `[0m[1;35mcmsFreeNamedColorList[0m[1;39m([0m[39mv[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Stack Buffer Overflow Fix** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom evaluation report[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The previous patch correctly addressed the buffer overflow by:[0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Directly addresses the leak**: Adding `nc2` cleanup to the Error label ensures[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall error paths properly free the allocated memory[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal code change**: Only adds one line of cleanup code, reducing risk of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows established patterns**: Mirrors the error handling in `SetTextTags` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand other functions in the codebase[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Safe NULL handling**: `cmsFreeNamedColorList` handles NULL pointers [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgracefully, so checking `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnc2 != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents any issues if Error is reached [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore `nc2` is allocated[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Success path unchanged**: The success path still frees `nc2` at line [0m[1;36m1107[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore returning[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **All error paths covered**: Every `goto Error` statement [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1076[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1084[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1087[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1091[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1098[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1106[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now properly cleans up `nc2`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No functional changes**: The fix only adds cleanup; it doesn't modify any [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbusiness logic[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Original not affected**: The fix doesn't touch `Original` since it's not owned[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the function[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Resolves the memory leak**: The [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m912[0m[39m bytes leaked [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m96[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m816[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from `nc2` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation will now be properly freed on error paths[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Maintains the buffer overflow fix**: All previous changes that fixed the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow are preserved[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Complete solution**: This addresses both the original issue and the new leak [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout introducing additional problems[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Side effect**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected - the change only adds proper cleanup on error [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Risk of double-free**: Mitigated by:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only freeing on error paths where the function returns NULL[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The success path still frees `nc2` at line [0m[1;36m1107[0m[39m as before[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No code path can reach both the success-path free and the error-path free[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Risk of use-after-free**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m - after freeing `nc2` in the Error label, the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction immediately returns NULL[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions from Codebase[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the exact pattern demonstrated in:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `SetTextTags` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m52[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m58[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Checks and frees each allocated resource[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `cmsAllocNamedColorList` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m764[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m767[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Frees on error during initialization[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `cmsDupNamedColorList` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m802[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Frees newly allocated structure on error[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe consistency with existing error handling patterns ensures maintainability and [0m  [2m                [0m
